i  (A)  adv.  (L.  magis);  i.  ever, 
or  never  ;  the  context  showing  how  it

un  fatto  simile,  such  a  thing  never  hap- 
pened before;  La  finirete  —  ?  will  you

-  piii  teatro,  no  more  gambling,  no 
more  theatre-going.  2.  It  may  express
